  \mbox{アク}, \mbox{オ} \\[2pt]%
  \mbox{あ.し}, \mbox{ああ}, \mbox{いずくに}, \mbox{いずくんぞ}, \mbox{にく.い}, \mbox{にく.む}, \mbox{わる}, \mbox{わる.い} \\[2pt]%

    %up to 6 compound meanings like '    \item [hiragana] [translation]'

\item わるい\\*

\item あく\\*

\item さいあく\\*

\item あくしつ\\*

\item あくま\\*
